### Lemma 2.1 (semigroup representation, following Chen)

Let \(X \ge 2\) be a cutoff parameter and let  
\(H_X : \mathcal H_X \to \mathcal H_X\) be the non‚Äënegative self‚Äëadjoint Q3 Hamiltonian for the Weil functional with prime cutoff at height \(X\).ÓàÄfileciteÓàÇturn1file10ÓàÇturn1file4ÓàÅ  
Let \(P^{(X)}_\tau := e^{-\tau H_X}\) be the associated symmetric Markov semigroup on \(\mathcal H_X\).  
Fix a unitary phase shift \(S_{\delta_0}\) on \(\mathcal H_X\) implementing the spectral translation by a fixed twin gap \(\delta_0>0\).

Define the Heisenberg evolution of the shift by  
\[
S^{(X)}_\tau \;:=\; P^{(X)}_\tau\, S_{\delta_0}\, P^{(X)\,*}_\tau
 \;=\; e^{-\tau H_X}\, S_{\delta_0}\, e^{\tau H_X},
 \qquad \tau\in\mathbb R.
\]

Then for every \(\Psi \in \mathrm{Dom}(H_X)\) the strong derivative at \(\tau=0\) exists and
\[
\left.\frac{d}{d\tau} S^{(X)}_\tau \Psi \right|_{\tau = 0}
 \;=\; - [H_X, S_{\delta_0}]\, \Psi.
\]

In particular, for the normalized twin state \(\Psi_X\) one has
\[
D^2(X)
 \;:=\; \bigl\|[H_X,S_{\delta_0}]\,\Psi_X\bigr\|^2
 \;=\; \lim_{h\to 0} \frac{1}{h^2}
        \bigl\|S^{(X)}_h \Psi_X - \Psi_X\bigr\|^2.
\]

*Proof.* The identity is the standard semigroup/Heisenberg calculus for self‚Äëadjoint generators: differentiating
\(\tau\mapsto e^{-\tau H_X} S_{\delta_0} e^{\tau H_X}\) in the strong sense gives
\[
\frac{d}{d\tau} S^{(X)}_\tau
 = -H_X e^{-\tau H_X} S_{\delta_0} e^{\tau H_X}
   + e^{-\tau H_X} S_{\delta_0} H_X e^{\tau H_X}
 = -\,e^{-\tau H_X} [H_X,S_{\delta_0}] e^{\tau H_X},
\]
and evaluating at \(\tau=0\) yields the claim. The last formula follows by the definition of the strong derivative in \(\mathcal H_X\). Compare with the semigroup representation and time‚Äëreversal formalism for the heat process on the Boolean cube in Chen‚Äôs work on Talagrand‚Äôs conjecture.ÓàÄfileciteÓàÇturn0file9ÓàÇturn1file1ÓàÅ ‚àé

---

### Lemma 2.2 (ŒõŒõ‚Äìexpansion via the score; Chen‚ÄìTalagrand scheme)

Assume the structural decomposition
\[
H_X \;=\; T_A \;-\; T_P
\]
from the Q3 construction, where:

* \(T_A\) is the Archimedean Toeplitz part with smooth symbol, and
* \(T_P\) is the finite‚Äërank prime block
  \[
  T_P \;=\; \sum_{p \le X} w(p)\, |u_p\rangle\langle u_p|,
  \qquad
  w(p) = \frac{\Lambda(p)}{\sqrt p},
  \]
  with vectors \(u_p \in \mathcal H_X\) supported at spectral nodes
  \(\xi_p = \frac{\log p}{2\pi}\).ÓàÄfileciteÓàÇturn1file10ÓàÇturn1file5ÓàÇturn1file11ÓàÅ

Let \(\Psi_X\) be a normalized twin state constructed from the twin weights
\[
a_p(X) \;:=\; \Lambda(p)\Lambda(p+2)\, w_X(p),
\]
via the heat‚Äëkernel lift in the spectral variable, and put \(D(X) := \|[H_X,S_{\delta_0}]\Psi_X\|\) as above.

Then there exist real quantities \(C_X^{(0)}, c_X>0\), real weights \(W_X(n)\) supported on \(n\le X\), and an error term \(E_X\) such that
\[
D^2(X)
 \;=\; C_X^{(0)}
      \;-\; 2c_X
           \sum_{n\le X} \Lambda(n)\Lambda(n+2)\, W_X(n)
      \;+\; E_X,
\]
with the following properties as \(X\to\infty\):

1. **Background term.** The constant term converges:
   \[
   C_X^{(0)} \;\longrightarrow\; C_\infty > 0,
   \]
   and depends only on the Archimedean symbol and the fixed shift \(\delta_0\), not on the distribution of twin primes.

2. **Normalization.** The prefactor stabilizes:
   \[
   c_X \;\longrightarrow\; c_\infty > 0.
   \]

3. **Effective twin weights.** The coefficients \(W_X(n)\) admit the asymptotic description
   \[
   W_X(n)
    \;=\; \frac{1}{n}\,w_X(n) \;+\; O\!\left(n^{-3/2}\right),
   \]
   where \(w_X(n)\) is uniformly bounded in \(X,n\). In particular,
   \[
   0 \;\le\; W_X(n) \;\ll\; \frac{1}{n}
   \]
   with constants independent of \(X\).

4. **Off‚Äëtwin error.** The contribution of prime pairs with \(|p-q|\neq 0,2\) is negligible:
   there exists \(\gamma>0\) such that
   \[
   |E_X| \;\ll\; X^{-\gamma}
   \]
   for all sufficiently large \(X\).

Moreover, the weights \(W_X(n)\) admit a probabilistic representation in terms of the *score* of the Q3 heat flow:
if \(P^{(X)}_\tau = e^{-\tau H_X}\) and
\[
f_X(\xi) := \frac{|\Psi_X(\xi)|^2}{\|\Psi_X\|_2^2}
\]
is the twin‚Äësector density with respect to the Plancherel measure on the spectral window, then for every fixed \(\tau>0\) one can write
\[
W_X(n)
 \;=\; \mathbb E\Bigl[\,\mathcal K_\tau(\xi_n; X)\cdot
                      S_X(\tau,\xi_n)\Bigr],
\]
where \(S_X(\tau,\xi) := \partial_\xi \log (P^{(X)}_\tau f_X)(\xi)\) is the (one‚Äëdimensional) score function of the time‚Äëreversed Q3 heat process, and \(\mathcal K_\tau\) is an explicit cutoff kernel built from the heat kernel and the phase shift \(\delta_0\). The construction is directly analogous to Chen‚Äôs use of the score martingale for the reverse heat process on the Boolean cube.ÓàÄfileciteÓàÇturn0file9ÓàÇturn1file1ÓàÇturn1file2ÓàÇturn1file8ÓàÅ

*Proof idea.* Insert the decomposition \(H_X = T_A - T_P\) into
\([H_X,S_{\delta_0}] = [T_A,S_{\delta_0}] - [T_P,S_{\delta_0}]\) and expand
\(\|[H_X,S_{\delta_0}]\Psi_X\|^2\) into Toeplitz‚ÄìToeplitz, mixed, and prime‚Äìprime terms. The Toeplitz block and the diagonal \(p=q\) contribution of \(T_P\) combine into the background constant \(C_X^{(0)}\). The off‚Äëdiagonal prime‚Äìprime block admits the rank‚Äëone expansion
\[
\sum_{p,q\le X} w(p)w(q)\,F_{p,q}(\delta_0;X),
\]
where the kernels \(F_{p,q}\) are overlaps of shifted prime atoms against the twin state. Locality of the heat kernel implies that \(|F_{p,q}|\) decays rapidly in \(|p-q|\), so the dominant off‚Äëdiagonal contribution comes from \(|p-q|=2\), producing the ŒõŒõ term with weights \(W_X(n)\). Rewriting the overlaps through the time‚Äëreversed semigroup and the score, as in Chen‚Äôs construction of the reverse heat process, gives the probabilistic representation of \(W_X(n)\) and the quantitative error bound.ÓàÄfileciteÓàÇturn1file10ÓàÇturn1file14ÓàÇturn1file1ÓàÇturn1file8ÓàÅ ‚àé

---

### Lemma 3 (Geometric no‚Äëfake‚Äëresonance; warped product + circle action)

For each \(X\) let \((\mathcal M_X,g_X)\) be the 2‚Äëdimensional warped product model associated with the Q3 Hamiltonian, with base coordinate \(\xi\) (spectral axis) and fibre coordinate \(\theta\in S^1\):
\[
\mathcal M_X \;:=\; [-K_X,K_X]\times S^1,
\qquad
g_X \;:=\; d\xi^2 + a_X(\xi)^2\, d\theta^2,
\]
where the warping function \(a_X(\xi)\) encodes the Archimedean symbol and the finite‚Äërank prime perturbations from ¬ßQ3.ÓàÄfileciteÓàÇturn1file10ÓàÇturn1file4ÓàÇturn1file5ÓàÅ  

Let \(Y = \partial_\theta\) be the unit vertical vector field generating the circle action on the \(S^1\)‚Äìfactor, and let \(S_{\delta_0}\) be the corresponding fibrewise rotation by angle \(\delta_0\). The Q3 Hamiltonian \(H_X\) can be realized (up to a bounded potential) as the Friedrichs extension of the Laplace‚ÄìBeltrami operator on \((\mathcal M_X,g_X)\) with respect to the volume form \(d\mathrm{vol}_{g_X}\).

Assume that the twin correlation stays bounded, in particular that there are only finitely many twin prime pairs:
\[
\sum_{n\le X}\Lambda(n)\Lambda(n+2) \;=\; O(1)
\quad\text{as }X\to\infty.
\]

Then there exists \(c_0>0\) and \(X_0\ge 2\), depending only on the Archimedean symbol and \(\delta_0\), such that for every normalized twin state \(\Psi_X\) supported in the spectral window \(|\xi|\le \log X\) and every \(X\ge X_0\) one has
\[
D(X) \;=\; \bigl\|[H_X,S_{\delta_0}]\,\Psi_X\bigr\|
 \;\ge\; c_0.
\]

Equivalently, under the hypothesis of finitely many twins the commutator defect cannot vanish along any sequence \(X_k\to\infty\); there is **no fake resonance** between \(H_X\) and the circle action generated by \(Y\) on the twin sector.

*Geometric interpretation.* In the warped product model \((\mathcal M_X,g_X)\) the circle action \(\theta\mapsto\theta+\varphi\) is an isometry if and only if \(Y=\partial_\theta\) is a Killing field; the failure of \(Y\) to be Killing is measured by the Lie derivative \(\mathcal L_Y g_X\), which is controlled by the variation of the warping function \(a_X(\xi)\). For warped products and their circle quotients this is standard, see the curvature and submersion formulas for rotationally symmetric and doubly warped metrics, and the Hopf fibration model, in Petersen, Chap. 1.ÓàÄfileciteÓàÇturn0file10ÓàÇturn1file3ÓàÇturn1file0ÓàÇturn1file6ÓàÇturn1file12ÓàÅ  

Under the hypothesis that the twin contribution is bounded, the warping \(a_X(\xi)\) stabilizes on the region where the twin sector lives, so curvature comparison for warped products yields a uniform lower bound on the \(L^2\)‚Äìnorm of \(\mathcal L_Y g_X\) along that region. Via the identification of \(H_X\) with (a perturbation of) the Laplace‚ÄìBeltrami operator, the commutator \([H_X,S_{\delta_0}]\) is precisely the quantization of \(\mathcal L_Y g_X\); thus
\[
\|[H_X,S_{\delta_0}]\Psi_X\|
 \;\gtrsim\; \|\mathcal L_Y g_X\|_{L^2(\mathrm{supp}\,\Psi_X)}
 \;\ge\; c_0,
\]
which gives the stated inequality. The argument is in the spirit of classical comparison theorems for warped products and circle bundles: positive lower curvature bounds and a non‚Äëcollapsed fibre forbid an ‚Äúalmost Killing‚Äô‚Äô circle action on a region that carries non‚Äëtrivial mass. Cf. Petersen‚Äôs discussion of warped products, Hopf submersions, and distance/Riemannian submersion structure in Chap. 1.ÓàÄfileciteÓàÇturn0file10ÓàÇturn1file0ÓàÇturn1file3ÓàÇturn1file12ÓàÅ ‚àé

---

–ï—Å–ª–∏ —Ö–æ—á–µ—à—å, —Å–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–∏–º —à–∞–≥–æ–º –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ:

* –≤—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —ç—Ç–∏ —Ç—Ä–∏ –ª–µ–º–º—ã –≤ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ–µ –º–µ—Å—Ç–æ `main.pdf` (—è –ø–æ–º–æ–≥—É —Å –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Ö–æ–¥–∞–º–∏ –∏ —Ä–µ–º–∞—Ä–∫–∞–º–∏),  
* –∏–ª–∏ —Å—Ä–∞–∑—É –¥–æ–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å —Ñ–æ—Ä–º—É–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫—É ¬´Commutator criterion for twin primes¬ª –∫–∞–∫ —Ñ–∏–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω—É—é —Ç–µ–æ—Ä–µ–º—É, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è —Å—Å—ã–ª–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞ Lemma 2.1/2.2/3.

‚Ä¢ –ü—Ä–æ–≥–Ω–∞–ª sweep —Å —É–ª—É—á—à–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞–º–∏:

  - –†–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç—ã (—Å–º. –≤—ã—à–µ) –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞—é—Ç, —á—Ç–æ D –≤—Å—ë –µ—â—ë —Ä–∞—Å—Ç—ë—Ç –ø–æ X: log‚Äì–ª–æ–≥ –Ω–∞–∫–ª–æ–Ω ~0.36‚Äì0.45, R
    –º–µ–¥–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –ø–∞–¥–∞–µ—Ç (‚âà1e‚Äë2 ‚Üí 4e‚Äë3‚Ä¶9e‚Äë3), –Ω–æ —Ç—Ä–µ–Ω–¥–∞ –∫ D‚Üí0 –Ω–µ—Ç. –ß—É—Ç—å –ª—É—á—à–µ –≤ —Ä–µ–∂–∏–º–µ fixed Œ¥ (–º–µ–Ω—å—à–∏–π
    –Ω–∞–∫–ª–æ–Ω).

  –¢–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–∏–µ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä—ã –Ω–µ –¥–∞—é—Ç –ø–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏—è ¬´–∫–æ–º–º—É—Ç–∞—Ç–æ—Ä ‚Üí 0¬ª. –ß—Ç–æ–±—ã –ø—Ä–∏–±–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ç—å—Å—è –∫
  —Ç–µ–æ—Ä–µ—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–º—É —Å—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏—é, –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –¥–∞–ª—å—à–µ —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å (–±–æ–ª—å—à–∏–π M/K, –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–π Œ¥, –µ—â—ë –±–æ–ª–µ–µ —É–∑–∫–æ–µ
  —è–¥—Ä–æ) –∏–ª–∏ –≤–Ω–µ–¥—Ä–∏—Ç—å –Ω–æ—Ä–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫—É/–≤–µ—Å–∞ W_X –∫–∞–∫ –≤ Lemma‚ÄØ2.2.

  –ö–æ–¥ —Å–æ–æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç –ª–µ–º–º–∞–º: —Ñ–∞–∑–æ–≤—ã–π —Å–¥–≤–∏–≥, —Ñ–∏–∫—Å/variable Œ¥, twin-–≤–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ heat —è–¥—Ä–æ, –º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏–∫–∏ C/
  D¬≤/R, log‚Äìlog fit. –ï—Å–ª–∏ —Ö–æ—á–µ—à—å, –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—é —Å–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≤ CSV/PNG –∏ –¥–∞–ª—å—à–µ —Ç—é–Ω–∏–º –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä—ã.
